### [236] [Quantization Impact on the Accuracy and Communication Efficiency Trade-off in Federated Learning for Aerospace Predictive Maintenance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08474)
*Abdelkarim Loukili*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在航空车队联邦学习中对轻量级CNN模型应用对称均匀量化的效果，发现在非独立同分布数据分布下，4位量化(INT4)在保持与32位浮点数(FP32)相当精度的同时，可将梯度通信成本降低8倍，而2位量化(INT2)则表现出不可接受的性能不稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在带宽有限的物联网节点上部署联邦学习时，梯度通信开销成为主要瓶颈。航空领域的预测性维护需要隐私保护，但现有的联邦学习方案在资源受限环境中的效率不足。

Method: 使用自定义设计的轻量级1-D卷积模型(AeroConv1D, 9,697参数)，在NASA C-MAPSS基准数据集上，通过联邦学习框架评估对称均匀量化(32、8、4、2位)对精度-效率权衡的影响。采用严格的多次随机种子评估(N=10)，对比了IID与非IID客户端数据划分的效果。

Result: INT4量化在FD001和FD002数据集上的精度与FP32统计上无显著差异(p值分别为0.341、0.264和0.534)，同时梯度通信量减少8倍(37.88KiB降至4.73KiB每轮)。IID分区低估了方差，非IID评估揭示了极端量化的不稳定性。INT2虽然在某些指标上表现较好，但存在灾难性的性能不稳定(变异系数CV=45.8% vs FP32的22.3%)。FPGA资源评估表明INT4可在Xilinx ZCU102上实现(85.5% DSP利用率)。

Conclusion: INT4量化是在航空联邦学习场景中实现高效通信的可行方案，能在保持精度的同时大幅降低通信开销。正确评估需使用现实中的非IID数据分布。INT2由于不可接受的性能不稳定性，不适合实际部署。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) enables privacy-preserving predictive maintenance across distributed aerospace fleets, but gradient communication overhead constrains deployment on bandwidth-limited IoT nodes. This paper investigates the impact of symmetric uniform quantization ($b \in \{32,8,4,2\}$ bits) on the accuracy--efficiency trade-off of a custom-designed lightweight 1-D convolutional model (AeroConv1D, 9\,697 parameters) trained via FL on the NASA C-MAPSS benchmark under a realistic Non-IID client partition. Using a rigorous multi-seed evaluation ($N=10$ seeds), we show that INT4 achieves accuracy \emph{statistically indistinguishable} from FP32 on both FD001 ($p=0.341$) and FD002 ($p=0.264$ MAE, $p=0.534$ NASA score) while delivering an $8\times$ reduction in gradient communication cost (37.88~KiB $\to$ 4.73~KiB per round). A key methodological finding is that naïve IID client partitioning artificially suppresses variance; correct Non-IID evaluation reveals the true operational instability of extreme quantization, demonstrated via a direct empirical IID vs.\ Non-IID comparison. INT2 is empirically characterized as unsuitable: while it achieves lower MAE on FD002 through extreme quantization-induced over-regularization, this apparent gain is accompanied by catastrophic NASA score instability (CV\,=\,45.8\% vs.\ 22.3\% for FP32), confirming non-reproducibility under heterogeneous operating conditions. Analytical FPGA resource projections on the Xilinx ZCU102 confirm that INT4 fits within hardware constraints (85.5\% DSP utilization), potentially enabling a complete FL pipeline on a single SoC. The full simulation codebase and FPGA estimation scripts are publicly available at https://github.com/therealdeadbeef/aerospace-fl-quantization.

</details>


### [237] [What Drives Representation Steering? A Mechanistic Case Study on Steering Refusal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08524)
*Stephen Cheng,Sarah Wiegreffe,Dinesh Manocha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究表明，通过激活修补框架发现，引导向量主要通过OV电路与注意力机制交互，而忽略QK电路，且引导向量可以大幅稀疏化而不影响性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然引导向量是大型语言模型对齐的有效技术，但缺乏对其工作原理的因果解释，特别是引导向量影响哪些内部机制以及如何导致不同模型输出的可解释性理解。

Method: 提出了多token激活修补框架，在拒绝案例中进行全面研究，分析引导向量在不同层次的功能性可互换电路，并将引导的OV电路进行数学分解。

Result: 发现引导向量主要通过OV电路与注意力机制交互，忽略QK电路；引导向量可以稀疏化90-99%仍保持大部分性能；不同引导方法在重要维度子集上具有一致性。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了引导向量在LLM对齐中的因果机制，证明了其稀疏化的可行性，为更高效的模型引导提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Applying steering vectors to large language models (LLMs) is an efficient and effective model alignment technique, but we lack an interpretable explanation for how it works-- specifically, what internal mechanisms steering vectors affect and how this results in different model outputs. To investigate the causal mechanisms underlying the effectiveness of steering vectors, we conduct a comprehensive case study on refusal. We propose a multi-token activation patching framework and discover that different steering methodologies leverage functionally interchangeable circuits when applied at the same layer. These circuits reveal that steering vectors primarily interact with the attention mechanism through the OV circuit while largely ignoring the QK circuit-- freezing all attention scores during steering drops performance by only 8.75% across two model families. A mathematical decomposition of the steered OV circuit further reveals semantically interpretable concepts, even in cases where the steering vector itself does not. Leveraging the activation patching results, we show that steering vectors can be sparsified by up to 90-99% while retaining most performance, and that different steering methodologies agree on a subset of important dimensions.

</details>

### [238] [MetaTele: Compact Refractive Metasurface Computational Telephoto Camera](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07614)
*Harshana Weligampola,Yuanrui Chen,Abhiram Gnanasambandam,Dilshan Godaliyadda,Hamid R. Sheikh,Stanley H. ChanQi Guo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能手机相机受制于光学放大倍率，传统折射光学难以将远摄比降至0.5以下而不引入多组笨重镜片校正像差。需要突破形式因素限制，实现紧凑型长焦成像。

Method: 1. 采用折衍混合光学组件：在窄波长带捕获精细结构图像，避免严重色差；2. 同一光学系统采集宽带色彩信息，虽有色差但保留足够光谱信息；3. 设计定制的一步扩散模型，将两种原始测量值融合，为结构图像着色并校正系统像差。

Result: 研制出MetaTele原型，在RGB成像中实现0.44的突破性远摄比，总轨道长度仅13毫米，首次在智能手机形态因素中达到单反级远摄能力。

Conclusion: MetaTele通过光学-算法协同设计，成功突破智能手机长焦成像的物理限制，为超紧凑高性能相机系统开辟了新途径，证明了折衍混合光学与计算成像结合的强大潜力。

Abstract: Smartphone cameras face fundamental form-factor constraints that limit their optical magnification, primarily due to the difficulty of reducing a lens assembly's telephoto ratio, the ratio between total track length (TTL) and effective focal length (EFL). Currently, conventional refractive optics struggle to achieve a telephoto ratio below 0.5 without requiring multiple bulky elements to correct optical aberrations. In this paper, we introduce MetaTele, a novel optics-algorithm co-design that breaks this bottleneck. MetaTele explicitly decouples the acquisition of scene structure and color information. First, it utilizes a compact refractive-metasurface optical assembly to capture a fine-detail structure image under a narrow wavelength band, inherently avoiding severe chromatic aberrations. Second, it captures a broadband color cue using the same optics; although this cue is heavily corrupted by chromatic aberrations, it retains sufficient spectral information to guide post-processing. We then employ a custom one-step diffusion model to computationally fuse these two raw measurements, successfully colorizing the structure image while correcting for system aberrations. We demonstrate a MetaTele prototype, achieving an unprecedented telephoto ratio of 0.44 with a TTL of just 13 mm for RGB imaging, paving the way for DSLR-level telephoto capabilities within smartphone form factors.

### [239] [A H.265/HEVC Fine-Grained ROI Video Encryption Algorithm Based on Coding Unit and Prompt Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08047)
*Xiang Zhang,Haoyan Lu,Ziqiang Li,Ziwen He,Zhenshan Tan,Fei Peng,Zhangjie Fu*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于CU和提示分割的细粒度ROI视频选择性加密算法，通过将加密单元精细化至8×8CU级别，解决了传统Tile级加密的精度不足问题，同时在预测过程中抑制加密扩散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有H.265/HEVC的ROI选择性加密方法通常以Tile（较大尺寸）作为最小加密单元，存在加密区域不精确、加密精度低的问题，难以应用于医疗、军事和遥感等敏感领域。

Method: 1. 提出基于提示分割的新型ROI映射方法，实现ROI到8×8CU级别的精确映射；
2. 设计基于多语法元素的选择性加密方案，扰动高精度ROI内的语法元素；
3. 采用PCM模式和MV限制的扩散隔离策略，处理预测过程中的加密扩散问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，该算法能够精确分割ROI区域，有效扰动区域内像素，消除加密引入的扩散伪影。

Conclusion: 该方法突破了现有ROI加密使用Tile的固有机制，将ROI视频加密的细粒度精度提升至最小8×8CU级别，在医疗影像、军事监控和偏远地区等领域具有广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: ROI (Region of Interest) video selective encryption based on H.265/HEVC is a technology that protects the sensitive regions of videos by perturbing the syntax elements associated with target areas. However, existing methods typically adopt Tile (with a relatively large size) as the minimum encryption unit, which suffers from problems such as inaccurate encryption regions and low encryption precision. This low-precision encryption makes them difficult to apply in sensitive fields such as medicine, military, and remote sensing. In order to address the aforementioned problem, this paper proposes a fine-grained ROI video selective encryption algorithm based on Coding Units (CUs) and prompt segmentation. First, to achieve a more precise ROI acquisition, we present a novel ROI mapping approach based on prompt segmentation. This approach enables precise mapping of ROIs to small $8\times8$ CU levels, significantly enhancing the precision of encrypted regions. Second, we propose a selective encryption scheme based on multiple syntax elements, which distorts syntax elements within high-precision ROI to effectively safeguard ROI security. Finally, we design a diffusion isolation based on Pulse Code Modulation (PCM) mode and MV restriction, applying PCM mode and MV restriction strategy to the affected CU to address encryption diffusion during prediction. The above three strategies break the inherent mechanism of using Tiles in existing ROI encryption and push the fine-grained level of ROI video encryption to the minimum $8\times8$ CU precision. The experimental results demonstrate that the proposed algorithm can accurately segment ROI regions, effectively perturb pixels within these regions, and eliminate the diffusion artifacts introduced by encryption. The method exhibits great potential for application in medical imaging, military surveillance, and remote areas.

Current state-of-the-art methods still rely on Generative Adversarial Networks (GANs) or standard convolutional U-Net diffusion models that often struggle with "structure and staining trade-offs". The generated samples are either structurally relevant but blurry, or texturally realistic but have artifacts that compromise their diagnostic use. In this paper, we introduce HistDiT, a novel latent conditional Diffusion Transformer (DiT) architecture that establishes a new benchmark for visual fidelity in virtual histological staining. The novelty introduced in this work is, a) the Dual-Stream Conditioning strategy that explicitly maintains a balance between spatial constraints via VAE-encoded latents and semantic phenotype guidance via UNI embeddings; b) the multi-objective loss function that contributes to sharper images with clear morphological structure; and c) the use of the Structural Correlation Metric (SCM) to focus on the core morphological structure for precise assessment of sample quality. Consequently, our model outperforms existing baselines, as demonstrated through rigorous quantitative and qualitative evaluations.

### [241] [DiV-INR: Extreme Low-Bitrate Diffusion Video Compression with INR Conditioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08329)
*Eren Çetin,Lucas Relic,Yuanyi Xue,Markus Gross,Christopher Schroers,Roberto Azevedo*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 提出一种基于隐式神经表示和预训练视频扩散模型的感知驱动超低码率视频压缩框架，在<0.05 bpp下显著提升感知质量指标


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对极低码率(<0.05 bpp)视频压缩场景，传统方法难以保持感知质量。INR提供紧凑表示但缺乏生成能力，扩散模型有丰富生成先验但需要有效引导，结合两者优势实现感知驱动压缩

Result: 在UVG、MCL-JCV等基准测试中，比HEVC在BD-LPIPS提升0.214、BD-FID提升91.14，优于VVC及现有神经编解码器，特别是在<0.05 bpp下感知指标(LPIPS、DISTS、FID)显著提升

Conclusion: INR条件扩散模型能分层压缩视频，先构建场景布局和物体识别，再细化纹理精度，这种语义到视觉的层次结构使极低码率下的感知保真压缩成为可能，为超低码率视频压缩提供了新方向

Abstract: We present a perceptually-driven video compression framework integrating implicit neural representations (INRs) and pre-trained video diffusion models to address the extremely low bitrate regime (<0.05 bpp). Our approach exploits the complementary strengths of INRs, which provide a compact video representation, and diffusion models, which offer rich generative priors learned from large-scale datasets. The INR-based conditioning replaces traditional intra-coded keyframes with bit-efficient neural representations trained to estimate latent features and guide the diffusion process. Our joint optimization of INR weights and parameter-efficient adapters for diffusion models allows the model to learn reliable conditioning signals while encoding video-specific information with minimal parameter overhead. Our experiments on UVG, MCL-JCV, and JVET Class-B benchmarks demonstrate substantial improvements in perceptual metrics (LPIPS, DISTS, and FID) at extremely low bitrates, including improvements on BD-LPIPS up to 0.214 and BD-FID up to 91.14 relative to HEVC, while also outperforming VVC and previous strong state-of-the-art neural and INR-only video codecs. Moreover, our analysis shows that INR-conditioned diffusion-based video compression first composes the scene layout and object identities before refining textural accuracy, exposing the semantic-to-visual hierarchy that enables perceptually faithful compression at extremely low bitrates.

</details>

### [242] [Tunneling-Augmented Simulated Annealing for Short-Block LDPC Code Construction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07365)
*Atharv Kanchi*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出了一个全局离散优化框架，通过直接优化奇偶校验矩阵来设计短分组线性码，在64-128分组长度上相比随机LDPC码获得了0.1-1.3 dB的信噪比增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 设计短分组长度的高性能纠错码对低延迟通信系统至关重要，因为解码性能由有限长度和图结构效应而非渐近特性决定。

Method: 将码设计表述为带有短循环、陷入集关联子结构和度数违规惩罚的约束二进制优化问题，采用隧道增强模拟退火与局部细化的混合策略探索非凸空间。

Result: 在AWGN信道上，64-128分组长度范围内相比随机LDPC码获得0.1-1.3 dB信噪比增益，平均增益为0.45 dB，性能与渐进边增长方法相差在0.6 dB以内。

Conclusion: 基于退火的全局优化可作为多目标约束下应用特定码设计的补充工具，但结构改进并不总是能带来解码增益。消除1906个陷入集模式仅导致+0.08 dB改进。

Abstract: Designing high-performance error-correcting codes at short blocklengths is critical for low-latency communication systems, where decoding is governed by finite-length and graph-structural effects rather than asymptotic properties. This paper presents a global discrete optimization framework for constructing short-block linear codes by directly optimizing parity-check matrices. Code design is formulated as a constrained binary optimization problem with penalties for short cycles, trapping-set-correlated substructures, and degree violations. We employ a hybrid strategy combining tunneling-augmented simulated annealing (TASA) with classical local refinement to explore the resulting non-convex space. Experiments at blocklengths 64-128 over the AWGN channel show 0.1-1.3 dB SNR gains over random LDPC codes (average 0.45 dB) and performance within 0.6 dB of Progressive Edge Growth. In constrained regimes, the method enables design tradeoffs unavailable to greedy approaches. However, structural improvements do not always yield decoding gains: eliminating 1906 trapping set patterns yields only +0.08 dB improvement. These results position annealing-based global optimization as a complementary tool for application-specific code design under multi-objective constraints.

</details>


### [243] [The Asymmetric Hamming Bidistance and Distributions over Binary Asymmetric Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07730)
*Shukai Wang,Cuiling Fan,Chunming Tang,Zhengchun Zhou*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文针对二进制不对称信道引入非对称汉明双距离及其分布，提出新的最大似然解码平均错误概率上界，并通过计算多种码族的完整分布展示了其应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源自实践中二进制不对称信道存在符号转变错误概率显著不同的特性，传统度量如重量分布和现有差异界在区分码的性能时存在局限，需要更精细的分析方法来准确评估最大似然解码性能。

Method: 提出非对称汉明双距离概念及其二维分布，分别捕捉码字间的方向差异；基于此推导最大似然解码平均错误概率新上界；计算包括双重量和三重量投影码、强正则图构造的码、对称平衡不完全区组设计非线性码等码族的完整非对称汉明双距离分布。

Result: 证明新推导的上界一般与Cotardo和Ravagnani提出的两个现有界不可比较；通过具体码族展示了非对称汉明双距离分布的完整计算方法和应用潜力。

Conclusion: 非对称汉明双距离提供了比传统度量更精细的码性能分析工具，新推导的上界为二进制不对称信道下最大似然解码性能评估提供了有价值的新视角，特别是在传统方法失效的场合具有明显优势。

Abstract: The binary asymmetric channel is a model for practical communication systems where the error probabilities for symbol transitions $0\rightarrow 1$ and $1\rightarrow0$ differ substantially. In this paper, we introduce the notion of asymmetric Hamming bidistance (AHB) and its two-dimensional distribution, which separately captures directional discrepancies between codewords. This finer characterization enables a more discriminative analysis of decoding the error probabilities for maximum-likelihood decoding (MLD), particularly when conventional measures, such as weight distributions and existing discrepancy-based bounds, fail to distinguish code performance. Building on this concept, we derive a new upper bound on the average error probability for binary codes under MLD and show that, in general, it is incomparable with the two existing bounds derived by Cotardo and Ravagnani (IEEE Trans. Inf. Theory, 68 (5), 2022). To demonstrate its applicability, we compute the complete AHB distributions for several families of codes, including two-weight and three-weight projective codes (with the zero codeword removed) via strongly regular graphs and 3-class association schemes, as well as nonlinear codes constructed from symmetric balanced incomplete block designs (SBIBDs).

</details>


### [244] [Modeling and Analysis for Joint Design of Communication and Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07735)
*Xu Gan,Chongjun Ouyang,Yuanwei Liu*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 作者提出了一个联合通信与控制设计（JDCC）的统一分析框架，定义了传输延迟与控制方差两个性能指标，推导了性能区域的帕累托边界。进一步通过MRT和ZF波束成形方法得到闭式解，并提出新的JDCC中断概率度量来评估系统可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物联网和智能控制系统中，通信质量与闭环控制性能紧密耦合，仅优化单一方面难以获得全局性能最优，因此需要建立统一的通信与控制联合设计框架，探索其基础性能边界和可靠性评估方法。

Method: 1) 建立JDCC统一分析框架，以传输延迟和稳态控制方差为性能指标；2) 导出通信与控制性能区域的帕累托边界；3) 分析最大比传输（MRT）和迫零（ZF）波束成形下的闭式解；4) 提出通信中断概率、控制中断概率及联合JDCC中断概率三个可靠性度量。

Result: 1) 帕累托边界有效刻画了JDCC系统的性能极限和通信与控制之间的权衡；2) 推导了MRT和ZF方案下各性能闭式表达式；3) 提出并验证了JDCC中断概率，发现系统可靠性受上下行闭环控制及其与通信耦合效应共同影响。

Conclusion: 该框架为JDCC系统提供了统一的分析基础，帕累托边界揭示了性能权衡的根本规律，JDCC中断概率可作为重要的可靠性评估工具。结果表明，必须同时考虑通信与控制之间的耦合关系才能实现系统最优性能与可靠性设计。

Abstract: A unified analytical framework for joint design of communication and control (JDCC) is proposed. Within this framework, communication transmission delay and steady-state control variance are derived as the two fundamental JDCC performance metrics. The Pareto boundary is then established to characterize the optimal communication-control trade-off in JDCC systems. To further obtain closed-form expressions, their performance regions are derived under maximum-ratio transmission (MRT) and zero-forcing (ZF) beamforming. For system reliability evaluation, the communication-only and control-only outage probabilities are first derived. Based on these, the JDCC outage probability is defined to quantify the probability that the communication-delay and control-error requirements cannot be simultaneously satisfied. Its analytical expressions are then derived under both MRT and ZF schemes. Finally, numerical results validate the theoretical results and reveal that: (1) the Pareto boundary characterizes the trade-off frontier and performance limit of JDCC systems and (2) the JDCC reliability is jointly determined by the uplink-downlink closed-loop control and its coupling with communication.

</details>


### [245] [Quantum Integrated Communication and Computing Over Multiple-Access Bosonic Channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08214)
*Ioannis Krikidis*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文研究了在相干态多址信道下，通过同时执行空中计算和多址数据解调的量子集成通信与计算方案


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子多址信道的叠加特性，实现通信与计算的联合设计，在保证通信速率的同时最大化计算精度，达到有效的计算-通信权衡

Method: 提出低复杂度交替优化框架，包括：1)接收系数的闭式线性最小均方误差更新；2)量子和速率约束的单调性利用；3)通信功率的投影梯度优化

Conclusion: 所提量子集成通信计算方案通过联合优化功率控制和接收系数，能在多址信道上同时支持空中计算和无线通信，为解决非凸优化问题提供了高效算法

Abstract: We investigate a quantum integrated communication and computation (QICC) scheme for a single-mode bosonic multiple-access channel (MAC) with coherent-state signalling. By exploiting the natural superposition property of the quantum MAC, a common receiver simultaneously performs over-the-air computation (OAC) on the analogue symbols transmitted by one set of devices and decodes multiple-access data from another. The joint design of the transmit power control and the receive coefficient leads to a non-convex optimization problem that maximizes computation accuracy under a prescribed sum-rate communication constraint. To address this challenge, we develop a low-complexity alternating-optimization framework that incorporates: (i) closed-form linear minimum-mean square error updates for the receive coefficient, (ii) monotonicity properties of the quantum sum-rate constraint, and (iii) projected-gradient refinements for the communication powers. The proposed QICC scheme achieves an effective computation-communication trade-off with fast convergence and low computational complexity.

</details>


### [246] [On the Capacity of Sequences of Coloring Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08234)
*Wenjun Yu,Moshe Schwartz*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 研究染色通道序列的精确容量，重点关注均匀向日葵、两相交集、路径等特定序列结构，通过构建配对图建立容量等价关系并给出上下界


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 染色通道序列在蛋白质识别和分子信息存储中有重要应用，理解其容量限制对设计有效的序列重构系统至关重要。当前缺乏对多种染色通道序列结构的系统性容量分析。

Method: 定义染色通道为允许特定字母子集通过、删除其他字母的通道。通过构建配对图将容量问题转化为图论问题，从而推导均匀向日葵、两相交集、路径等结构的精确容量，并设计适用于循环结构的定制界限。

Result: 获得了几类染色通道序列的精确容量，建立了容量与配对图的等价关系，证明了容量的上下界，并对4字母表下的循环长度4序列给出了具体界限（未能获得精确容量）。

Conclusion: 染色通道序列的容量可由配对图完全刻画，该理论框架为分析更复杂序列结构提供了基础，但仍需进一步研究循环等特定结构的精确容量计算问题。

Abstract: A single coloring channel is defined by a subset of letters it allows to pass through, while deleting all others. A sequence of coloring channels provides multiple views of the same transmitted letter sequence, forming a type of sequence-reconstruction problem useful for protein identification and information storage at the molecular level. We provide exact capacities of several sequences of coloring channels: uniform sunflowers, two arbitrary intersecting sets, and paths. We also show how this capacity depends solely on a related graph we define, called the pairs graph. Using this equivalence, we prove lower and upper bounds on the capacity, and a tailored bound for a coloring-channel sequence forming a cycle. In particular, for an alphabet of size $4$, these results give the exact capacity of all coloring-channel sequences except for a cycle of length $4$, for which we only provide bounds.

</details>


### [247] [On quadratic binomial vectorial functions with maximal bent components](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08311)
*Xianhong Xie,Yi Ouyang,Shenxing Zhang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文研究了具有最大数量bent分量的二项向量函数F(x)=x^{d_1}+x^{d_2}在特定条件下的性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有最大bent分量数量的二项向量函数的分类，探讨其代数性质与密码学特性之间的联系。这类函数在密码学中具有重要意义，因为bent函数具有最优的非线性性。

Method: 通过分析2-adic Hamming重量、Frobenius自同构和代数扩张等代数工具，研究了二项向量函数的结构特性。使用了等价类分析和图像集基数方法来推导非线性度和差分均匀性的界限。

Result: 证明了在特定条件下，具有最大bent分量数量且2-adic Hamming重量不超过2的二项向量函数要么等价于x^{2^m+1}，要么等价于x^{2^i}(x+x^{2^m})。同时建立了基于图像集基数的非线性度和差分均匀性的界限。

Conclusion: 该研究为具有最大bent分量数量的二项向量函数提供了完整的分类结果，并建立了这类函数的重要密码学性质界限，对密码学函数设计有指导意义。

Abstract: Assume $n=2m\geq 2$ and let $F(x)=x^{d_1}+x^{d_2}$ be a binomial vectorial function over $\F_{2^n}$ possessing the maximal number (i.e. $2^n-2^m$) of bent components. Suppose the $2$-adic Hamming weights $\wt_2(d_1)$ and $\wt_2(d_2)$ are both at most $2$, we prove that $F(x)$ is affine equivalent to either $x^{2^m+1}$ or $x^{2^i}(x+x^{2^m})$, provided that \[
  \ell(n):=\min_{γ:~\F_2(γ)=\F_{2^n}} \dim_{\F_2}\F_2[σ]γ>m, \] where $σ$ is the Frobenius $(x\mapsto x^2)$ on $\F_{2^n}$, and $\gcd(d_1,d_2,2^m-1)>1$. Under this condition, we also establish two bounds on the nonlinearity and the differential uniformity of $F$ by means of the cardinality of its image set.

</details>


### [248] [Power Amplifier-aware Power Allocation for Noise-limited and Distortion-limited Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08437)
*Achref Tellili,Nathaniel Paul Epperson,Mohamed Akrout*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 传统注水功率分配基于PA线性工作假设，本文直接整合PA非线性特性，利用Bussgang定理构建统计线性化模型，提出投影梯度下降算法优化功率分配和空间回退策略，推导出区分噪声受限与失真受限工作机制的闭式阈值，在饱和区域相比标准注水法获得显著容量增益


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统注水功率分配策略假设功放工作在线性区域，但在实际应用中功放常在接近饱和的非线性区域工作，导致失真噪声不可忽略。为移除线性假设并能在失真噪声显著的工作机制下优化系统性能，需要将功放非线性特性直接纳入功率分配设计中

Method: 1) 利用Bussgang定理对功放硬限幅模型进行统计线性化，刻画信号增益与功率相关失真之间的权衡关系；2) 提出投影梯度下降算法，在优化功率分配的同时确定最优空间回退策略；3) 推导闭式热噪声方差阈值，根据失真噪声方差和信道Frobenius范数区分噪声受限和失真受限工作机制

Result: 数值仿真验证了所提出的放大器感知策略在饱和机制下相比标准注水法能提供显著的容量增益，特别是在功放工作在非线性区域时表现优异

Conclusion: 本文通过将功放非线性直接整合到功率分配公式中，开发了一种能够在不线性假设条件下工作的功率分配策略，在失真噪声不可忽略的饱和机制下实现了容量性能的提升，为实际射频系统中的功放非线性补偿提供了有效解决方案

Abstract: The conventional power allocation strategy via water-filling relies on the premise that the power amplifier (PA) operates sufficiently below saturation such that a linear RF chain model holds. This work integrates the PA nonlinearity directly into the power allocation formulation, thereby removing the linearity assumption altogether and enabling operation in regimes where distortion noise is non-negligible. Leveraging the Bussgang theorem, we establish a statistical linearization of the PA's hard-limiting model to characterize the trade-off between signal gain and power-dependent distortion. We propose a projected gradient descent algorithm that optimizes power allocation while identifying an optimal spatial back-off strategy. We also derive a closed-form thermal noise variance threshold that separates the noise-limited and distortion-limited operating regimes as a function of the distortion noise variance and the channel Frobenius norm. Numerical simulations validate that our amplifier-aware strategy provides significant capacity gains in the saturation regime compared to standard water-filling.

</details>


### [249] [Formalizing building-up constructions of self-dual codes through isotropic lines in Lean](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08485)
*Jae-Hyun Baek,Jon-Lark Kim*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文展示了Kim的二进制自对偶码构建方法与Chinburg-Zhang的希尔伯特符号构造的等价性，并引入q元版本的高效构造方法，应用于多进制自对偶码的构建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究不同自对偶码构造方法之间的内在联系，发展更高效的多进制自对偶码构造技术，解决q元情况下的扩展问题。

Method: 通过三种互补视角研究分裂有限域上的自对偶码：构建-扩展构造、Chinburg-Zhang的二进制算术约简、欧几里得平面的双曲几何。利用生成矩阵的高效形式和分裂盒状构造。

Result: 证明了两种构造方法的等价性；构造了多进制最优自对偶码，包括GF(5)上的[6,3,4]和[8,4,4]码、GF(13)上的MDS自对偶[8,4,5]和[10,5,6]码，以及GF(13)上的[12,6,6]码。

Conclusion: 不同构造方法在代数条件下存在统一联系，新方法能高效构造多进制最优自对偶码，理论结果已通过Lean 4形式化验证。

Abstract: The purpose of this paper is two-fold. First we show that Kim's building-up construction of binary self-dual codes is equivalent to Chinburg-Zhang's Hilbert symbol construction. Second we introduce a $q$-ary version of Chinburg-Zhang's construction in order to construct $q$-ary self-dual codes efficiently. For the latter, we study self-dual codes over split finite fields \(\F_q\) with \(q \equiv 1 \pmod{4}\) through three complementary viewpoints: the building-up construction, the binary arithmetic reduction of Chinburg--Zhang, and the hyperbolic geometry of the Euclidean plane. The condition that \(-1\) be a square is the common algebraic input linking these viewpoints: in the binary case it underlies the Lagrangian reduction picture, while in the split \(q\)-ary case it produces the isotropic line governing the correction terms in the extension formulas. As an application of our efficient form of generator matrices, we construct optimal self-dual codes from the split boxed construction, including self-dual \([6,3,4]\) and \([8,4,4]\) codes over \(\GF{5}\), MDS self-dual \([8,4,5]\) and \([10,5,6]\) codes over \(\GF{13}\), and a self-dual \([12,6,6]\) code over \(\GF{13}\). These structural statements are accompanied by a Lean~4 formalization of the algebraic core.

</details>
